< review>
Very grateful to Marco, David Y., and the team at Handy Plumbing Man! I'd been calling around looking for someone to help with a backed up main line, which was affecting my apartment and the neighbors' place. The pressure had caused the wax seal around my toilet to break -- so there was dirty toilet water leaking all over my bathroom floor. The first place I called said they couldn't do anything beyond a localized stoppage (basically all they can do is plunge your toilet for you, apparently?!). Then I called another place that was like "let me look at our schedule and get back to you" -- no call back for over an hour. So I was frantic to find someone. What a different with Marco! He answered right away and immediately reassured me that they could handle it and then got us on the schedule. David Y was on the site within an hour of the call, and had fixed everything before noon. Don't waste your time with other plumbing outfits like I did. Save yourself the time and anxiety and start here!! So grateful to their expertise, patience, and professionalism.< /review>

<userid>113311233474726466889</userid><Name>Alan Walworth<//Name><time>1621103690199< /time><Rating>5< /Rating>< text>
In attempting to replace my kitchen sink's leaky pull-out sprayer hose, I broke the hard to turn shut-off valves under the sink when applying some force to turn them to the closed position. When I turned them back on (after deciding to postpone the hose replacement pending investigation of how to take apart the hose connection, the pieces of which did not easily come apart as expected), the kitchen sink water when turned on full only dripped out slightly. Fortunately, these angle stop valves are designed to break in such a way that water does not flow through them. (Lesson learned: shut-off valves under sinks should be exercised occasionally to help them continue to function properly---several years without use can make them malfunction.)

Dave from Handy Plumbing was able to come the next day and replace the valves for a price agreed on in advance of the visit. He helpfully installed the new pull-out hose for us without any additional charge. Based on this very positive experience I recommend Handy Plumbing;  they will be our first choice for future plumbing needs.< /text>

<rating>5<//rating><pics>None</pics><text>This isn't a review for one visit, but an overall experience with this location.  Our family has been a Round Table Pizza customer for the past 20+ years.  We've been going to this location for almost five years now.  We usually rotate between three or four different pizzas since we have multiple favorites.  The wings are great**, and much bigger than a wingstop Chicken wing.  My wife loves the Garlic Twists.  They are pizza dough, garlic, cheese, and a ranch(?) type sauce cooked to order.  The pizza is a bit more expensive than a Domino's/Papa John's/Little Caesar's, but the quality is MUCH better.  If you usually get cheap pizza, do yourself a favor and try Round Table.

Edit:  They changed the size of their pizzas.  The large used to be 16 slices, but is now 12.  The extra large is 16 slices but used to be 20.  There doesn't seem to be a 20 slice pizza anymore.  They also changed the wings when I wasn't paying attention.  I do not recommend the boneless wings.  Haven't tried the Classic wings since they made the change.  My rating has gone from five stars to four.  It used to be expensive but worth it.  The ingredients are still incredible, but the bang for your buck has diminished substantially.< /text>< user>

After reading the negative reviews below, I was somewhat reluctant to visit this store. However my experience today was absolutely the opposite.  I wanted to learn more of the Banner brand --  as the mattresses are locally made(so they say) --  and wanted to compare other brands on a new queen. < review>
I am a real person who has lived in the Coachella Valley for 28 years . I own a business which requires me to be on my feet most of the day. I have been living with chronic pain in my lower back for the last 12 years and by the end of my workday, it is difficult to bend down, reach out in front of me, get out of my car, or lift anything without pain.

I spent the last 6 months reviewing mattresses and to be honest, I was completely confused! There's NO WAY you can buy a mattress without laying on it to get the feel for the firmness or comfort you personally like.
I went to Banner Mattress in La Quinta with full intentions of shopping other mattress stores that evening.

I was greeted by a gentleman named "Octavio" who assisted me the entire time . He was not pushy but was extremely informative. He explained the springs in each mattress I tested, the fabrics, the coolness level, and all information relating to each level of comfort, firmness and support from each companies mattress.

I ended up buying the first mattress I tested but not until I had laid on every mattress in the store!  I purchased the Scorziell  Amalfi brand pillow top which I found out is Banner Mattresses signature brand.    I am telling the truth that I have spoken to Octavio twice now since I purchased the bed.... I have had  NO BACK PAIN  SINCE THE BED WAS DELIVERED!!!!
My husband has not put an ice pack on his back since our new mattress arrived !!!!!

Octavio was professional, courteous, knowledgeable and "tuned in" to my needs.
Thank you so much for guiding me and helping me relieve years of back pain! We are very happy with Banner Mattress and Octavio, a true professional!

Kytti St. Amand< /review>

<Rating>5< /Rating>< review>
I purchased a new Mazda CX-5 from another dealer a few weeks ago, and yesterday noticed a clicking sound from one of the tires. When I inspected it, there was a nail puncturing the tire. I brought in my car to Culver City Mazda since it's actually the closest dealer to where I live.

They couldn't find a record of the pricey service plan that should cover this repair (I have to call the original dealer about this), but Ken in the service department offered to inspect it to see if it's something repairable.

It was really a great experience, and if the purpose was to bring me back the next time I need service, it definitely worked. Everyone was very courteous and professional.  I brought it in early on a weekday morning and all in all it took about an hour which I felt was reasonable.

< review>
While shopping for a Mazda CX-5, someone in the business recommended that I meet with Tony, the fleet manager at the Culver City Mazda location. When I made an appointment to meet with him, he blew me off and had me work with one of his associates, which was fine because I know they‚Äôre busy. I met with Rosie, who truly created a great experience. She was professional, knowledgeable, and nice to work with. After two test drives, I was ready to buy the car. I found a better deal at a different location, but because Rosie had put time and effort into the sale, I gave her an opportunity to earn the commission by countering the deal. She said she could beat the price by $300 and threw in a due bill for Apple CarPlay and some curtesy rubber mats. After inspecting the car, which was excellently detailed, I was ready to pull the trigger and sign some paperwork. I met with Richard, the Finance Manager of F&I. Initially, I found him to also be professional and courteous, but he quickly revealed himself as a misogynist who attempted to take advantage of me as a woman and first time car buyer. He quoted me at 6% interest rate, which you know is absurd if you‚Äôre familiar with how financing works. I was putting down more than half of the car‚Äôs worth and have a fairly decent credit score (680 with trans union and 733 with Equifax). He repeatedly called me ‚Äúsweetie‚Äù and told me that there was nothing he could do to reduce the interest rate and that only the bank can do that, which was clearly untrue. After telling him that I was leaving, he left to ‚Äúget approval‚Äù from the fleet manager to lower my interest rate. I thought only the banks could do that? He then gave me an interest rate just under 4%. When I told him that was still ridiculous and I was leaving, he said ‚Äúsweetie, you just don‚Äôt understand how all of this works.‚Äù They clearly were not going to give me a reasonable interest rate, so I asked about leasing instead because I know that Mazda has a 0% interest rate for leasing. Tony and Richard gave me the worst quote I‚Äôve ever heard of in my life. Putting $6,000 down to pay $300 a month for a MAZDA is absurd. They very obviously did not want my business, so I left. They offered me a 2.4% interest rate and I gave my business to them instead. Claudia Campos was my salesperson and she was phenomenal, as was the finance manager Paris. It was a smooth process and I drove off the lot last night.
